                jQuery(document).ready(function(){

                        enableMigration = function() {
                            if(! jQuery.fn.dialog) {
                                // THIS IS AWFUL - We currently cannot load jquery UI due to the maddening fact that it is already loaded
                                // multiple times with different versions as is Jquery.  Dialog is sometimes loaded and sometimes not
                                // depending on the speed I guess at which scripts load and then jQuery is being redefined at the end
                                // so depending on when this code executes it may or may not be defined and we cannot even consistently
                                // count on it being defined at the end because the jQuery reference is being redefined at some point
                                // during the load process.
                                //
                                // Also if we try to load it now with a jQuery getScript this breaks other jQuery UI functionality that
                                // is loaded piecemeal in different versions already so draggable breaks and other things as well could
                                // break.
                                //
                                // So here it goes the ugliest hack I can think of.  Manually define dialog and it's missing dependencies.

eventName:'com.cobaltgroup.ws.view.page',
handler:function(eventName, publisherData, subscriberData) {
function setCookie() {
	var exdate=new Date();
	exdate.setDate(exdate.getDate() + 365);
	document.cookie="cbltEdmunds=true; expires="+exdate.toUTCString();
}

function getCookie(c_name) {
	var i,x,y,ARRcookies=document.cookie.split(";");
	for (i=0;i<ARRcookies.length;i++) {
		x=ARRcookies[i].substr(0,ARRcookies[i].indexOf("="));
		y=ARRcookies[i].substr(ARRcookies[i].indexOf("=")+1);
		x=x.replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g,"");
		if (x==c_name) {
			return unescape(y);
		}
	}
}

function runEdmunds() {
	window._edw = {"account":"cblt8275", "data":{}};
	var edw = document.createElement('script'); 
	edw.type = 'text/javascript'; 
	edw.async = true;
	edw.src = 'http://static.ed.edmunds-media.com/edmunds-webassets/current/wro/edw-partner-cblt8275.js';
	var s = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0]; 
	s.parentNode.insertBefore(edw, s);
}

function checkEdmunds() {
	var tagged=getCookie("cbltEdmunds");
	if (tagged==null || tagged=="") {
		setCookie();
		runEdmunds();
	}
}

checkEdmunds();
},
source:'Edmunds'
